At	least	four	people	have	been	shot	dead	in	two	suspected	political	attacks	in	South	Africa	's	volatile	Zulu	heartland	,	police	said	on	Friday	.
IN	JJS	CD	NNS	VBP	VBN	VBN	JJ	IN	CD	VBN	JJ	NNS	IN	NNP	NNP	POS	JJ	NNP	NN	,	NN	VBD	IN	NNP	.
